environment:
The geographical environment of the hotel is surrounded by mountains and rivers, which is indeed very good. It is good to stay away from the city and just breathe oxygen. The temperature difference between these two days is huge. In the morning, you can see the smoky fairyland scene, which is very beautiful. The small waterfall in the hotel park has a large amount of water and is worth a visit.
The facilities in the room are relatively complete. There is a bathtub and disposable bathing equipment on the balcony for free use, but it was not used because it was cold at night. In addition, there are several choices of pillows. You can ask at the counter according to your needs. There is free water and soda in the refrigerator, which will be replenished in time the next day.
Manager Leon was attentive and courteous. At that time, we only saw two pick-up and drop-off services. After feedback to the other party, the manager said that we can directly contact the counter to enjoy multiple services! Very cool! It was convenient for us to go to Sakura Park the next day. In addition, we were given exquisite fruits and delicious specialty sesame cakes to taste. Thank you so much!

Parts that need improvement: It would be better if the types of hot springs could be more abundant. We didn't seem to see the sauna. We were rushing to take a steaming bath after soaking in the hot springs, but we didn't find it.

msg:Transportation: I choose to drive by myself. It takes 3.5 hours from Panyu, Guangzhou to arrive. If you want to take the high-speed rail, you can book a pick-up with the hotel in advance. There are Tesla (2 yuan per kilowatt hour) and Xiaopeng charging piles in the hotel, which can be charged upon arrival.

Eating: I arrived at 21:00 in the evening, so I checked in first, let the children eat some snacks prepared with me, and went to bathe in the hot spring (the hot spring area ends at 23:30). After soaking in the hot spring, I ordered the dry-fried beef river from the hotel restaurant (the taste was great). I didn't feel good about the beef and mutton skewers. There was a 15% service charge for late night snacks (acceptable). Breakfast is a buffet with a wide variety of fruits, fresh fruits, and delicious bread. I feel that breakfast is pretty much the same. After soaking in the hot springs, you can eat farm food in the surrounding area in the afternoon. You must try the fish from the reservoir here. After all, the fish is very delicious due to the beautiful scenery.

Service: Both the hotel area front desk and the hot spring area front desk are pretty good. They gave me a room closer to the hot spring area when they saw that I had a baby. Toothbrushes, slippers, and bath towels were delivered quickly after calling for supplies. The staff in the hot spring area are also very good, smiling and chatting throughout the process. There is a free food court in the hot spring area to provide energy replenishment.
	
Water quality: Real hot spring water. We played with it for a long time without soaking our fingers. The staff will change the water in the morning. The water temperature of the hot spring pool is always within 45 degrees. I asked the staff in the children's playground area that there is no warm water from Monday to Friday. On Saturdays and Sundays, the water temperature will be within 35 degrees. In fact, it was not bad, because I had been soaking in hot springs and my body was very hot, so I asked Xiaobao to go to the cold water area and play for a while.
	
Shaoguan Ruyuan has beautiful mountains and rivers, and is relatively close to Danxia Mountain. It is worth visiting twice or three times. The duty manager Leon's service is very attentive and thoughtful, thank you.
